<p>PW Conductivity dan PW Conductivity action limit : Sesuai Lampiran
SOP/EBI/EN-015-L07</p>
<p>UV Lamp hour meter alert limit : 8000 h, UV Lamp hour meter action
limit : 8500 h</p>
<p>PW Loop Flow Velocity alert limit : 1.1 m/s, PW Loop Flow Velocity
action limit : 1 m/s</p>
<p>Pressure Diff. of 5 micron filter alert limit : 6 psi</p>
<p>Pressure Diff. of 5 micron filter action limit : 7 psi</p>
<p>Pembuatan NaOH dan NaClO mengacu pada SOP/EBI/EN-015. point 7.1.1.2
dan 7.1.1.3.</p></td>

limit : 8500 h</p>

<td colspan="5" style="text-align: center;"><p>Notes :</p>
<p>PW Conductivity dan PW Conductivity action limit : Sesuai Lampiran
SOP/EBI/EN-015-L07</p>
<p>UV Lamp hour meter alert limit : 8000 h, UV Lamp hour meter action
limit : 8500 h</p>
<p>PW Loop Flow Velocity alert limit : 1.1 m/s, PW Loop Flow Velocity
action limit : 1 m/s</p>
<p>Pressure Diff. of 5 micron filter alert limit : 6 psi</p>

<p>Pembuatan NaOH dan NaClO mengacu pada SOP/EBI/EN-015. point 7.1.1.2
dan 7.1.1.3.</p></td>

action limit : 1 m/s</p>
